class pod {
    is30DayMonth(month: number) {
        return [4, 5, 9, 11].includes(month)
    }

    @mem day(v?: number) {
        if (v && v > 30 && this.is30DayMonth(this.month()) ) throw new Error()

        return v ?? 1
    }

    @mem month(v?: number) {
        if (v && this.is30DayMonth(v) && this.day() > 30) throw new Error()

        return v ?? 1
    }
}
